style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">CB&amp;I Reports 2015 Second Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:3px;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">New Awards and Mozambique LNG Enhance Long-term Backlog Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">THE WOODLANDS, Texas, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">July 23, 2015 /PRNewswire/ --&#160;CB&amp;I (NYSE: CBI) today reported the second quarter resulted in strong earnings, improved cash flow and consistent operating performance. Net income for the second quarter was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$169.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$1.55</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;per diluted share, an increase of 14 percent from adjusted net income for the comparable period in 2014. Revenues were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$3.2 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, including a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$240 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;negative impact attributable to the translation effect of the strong dollar. Net cash provided by operating activities during the second quarter was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$95 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">. New awards for the second quarter totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$2.8 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, and new awards for the first six months totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$5.9 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">. Backlog remained fairly constant at nearly </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$29.4 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, including an adverse foreign exchange impact of $270 million year to date. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">During the quarter, CB&amp;I and its joint venture partners Chiyoda Corporation and Saipem were selected by Anadarko Petroleum Corporation to design and construct process and ancillary infrastructure associated with its LNG development program in Mozambique. CB&amp;I expects to book its share of the initial phase of the project in the fourth quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">"We continue to deliver solid performance despite a volatile commodity market and geopolitical issues that create instability in many of the traditional international energy markets," said Philip K. Asherman, CB&amp;I&#8217;s President and Chief Executive Officer. "The U.S. remains a great opportunity for us particularly in LNG, petrochemicals and fossil power generation markets. East Africa will be a source of solid backlog for many years as Anadarko and other owners develop these tremendous assets. Additionally, we continue to produce significant profitability from not only our insourcing capabilities but also the diverse portfolio of new opportunities in our facilities maintenance, engineered products, steel plate storage, pipe fabrication, technology licensing and catalyst businesses."</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:10px;padding-top:6px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Other significant awards for the second quarter include a combined-cycle gas turbine power project in the U.S., multiple maintenance services awards in North and South America, engineered products in Russia and Mexico, scope increases for our large nuclear projects in the U.S., and a variety of technology and fabrication awards globally.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Earnings Conference Call</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">CB&amp;I will host a webcast on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">July 23</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;at 4:00 p.m. Central time (5:00 p.m. Eastern time) to discuss financial and operating results and answer questions from investors. The webcast will be available on the Investor Relations page of www.cbi.com.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">About CB&amp;I </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">CB&amp;I (NYSE:CBI) is the most complete energy infrastructure focused company in the world. With 125 years of experience and the expertise of approximately 54,000 employees, CB&amp;I provides reliable solutions while maintaining a relentless focus on safety and an uncompromising standard of quality. For more information, visit www.cbi.com.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sAB6CCAFD1269CACF661676E7D73E6E68"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Important Information For Investors And Shareholders</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">This press release contains forward-looking statements regarding CB&amp;I and represents our expectations and beliefs concerning future events.
